[30;1m262 | [0m[35m                # child sensor C. Calling record on C would cause a record on[0m
[30;1m263 | [0m[35m                # P as well. So expiration time for P == expiration time for C.[0m
[30;1m264 | [0m[35m                # If the record on P happens via C just after P is removed,[0m
[30;1m265 | [0m[35m                # that will cause C to also get removed. Since the expiration[0m
[30;1m266 | [0m[35m                # time is typically high it is not expected to be a significant[0m
